When the player or an enemy steps into a blood puddle, bloody boot footprints appear behind them, becoming more transparent with each step until they disappear.\n\n### Key Features\n- **Blood puddle detection**: Characters detect when they step in blood via Area2D overlap\n- **Fading footprints**: Each consecutive footprint is more transparent than the previous\n- **Persistent decals**: Footprints do NOT fade over time (as per requirements)\n- **Unlimited count**: No maximum limit on footprints (as per requirements)\n- **Both characters**: Feature applies to both player and enemies\n- **Alternating feet**: Left/right foot alternation for realistic trail\n- **Facing direction rotation**: Footprints rotate based on character's facing direction (aim direction)\n\n### Technical Implementation\n- New `BloodyFeetComponent` component attached to Player and Enemy scenes\n- New `BloodFootprint.tscn` scene for footprint decals\n- Updated `BloodDecal` script to add Area2D collision for puddle detection\n- Added unit tests for `BloodyFeetComponent`\n\n### Configuration (BloodyFeetComponent)\n| Property | Default | Description |\n|----------|---------|-------------|\n| `blood_steps_count` | 6 | Number of footprints before blood runs out |\n| `step_distance` | 30.0 | Pixels between footprint spawns |\n| `initial_alpha` | 0.8 | Alpha of first footprint |\n| `alpha_decay_rate` | 0.12 | Alpha reduction per step |\n| `footprint_scale` | 0.8 | Size multiplier for footprints |\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n#### Session 1 (2026-01-25)\n\n1. **C# Player Scene Missing Component**: The `BloodyFeetComponent` was only added to the GDScript Player scene, but `BuildingLevel.tscn` uses the C# Player scene (`scenes/characters/csharp/Player.tscn`). Added the component to the C# scene.\n\n2. **Blood Detector Not Following Character**: The Area2D blood detector was parented to the `BloodyFeetComponent` Node (which has no transform), causing it to stay at world position (0, 0) instead of following the character. Fixed by parenting the detector to the CharacterBody2D.\n\n#### Session 2 (2026-01-25)\n\n3. **Texture Cropping Issue**: Boot print textures (11x16 px) were being cropped at top/bottom when rotated. Added vertical padding by increasing texture height to 20px (11x20).\n\n4. **Footprint Rotation Direction**: Footprints were rotating based on movement direction instead of character facing direction. Now uses `PlayerModel` or `EnemyModel` global_rotation to match the direction the character is looking/aiming. Handles flipped sprites correctly (when aiming left, scale.y is negative).\n\n### Debug Logging\n- Enabled `debug_logging = true` in scene files for testing\n- Added logging to `blood_decal.gd` for tracing puddle creation\n- Added periodic overlap check logging to `BloodyFeetComponent`\n\n### Files Changed\n- `scripts/components/bloody_feet_component.gd` - Main component (facing direction rotation)\n- `scripts/effects/blood_footprint.gd` - Footprint decal script\n- `scenes/effects/BloodFootprint.tscn` - Footprint scene\n- `scripts/effects/blood_decal.gd` - Added puddle detection Area2D + logging\n- `scenes/characters/Player.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent (GDScript version)\n- `scenes/characters/csharp/Player.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent (C# version)\n- `scenes/objects/Enemy.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent\n- `assets/sprites/effects/boot_print_*.png` - Boot print textures (11x20 with padding)\n- `tests/unit/test_bloody_feet_component.gd` - Unit tests\n- `docs/case-studies/issue-360/` - Case study with debugging analysis and game logs\n\n## Test plan\n\n- [ ] Player stepping in blood puddle triggers footprint spawning\n- [ ] Footprints fade in alpha with each step (not over time)\n- [ ] Footprints stop appearing after `blood_steps_count` steps\n- [ ] Stepping in blood again resets the footprint counter\n- [ ] Enemies also leave bloody footprints\n- [ ] Footprints rotate to match character facing direction (not movement)\n- [ ] Texture not cropped at top/bottom when rotated\n- [ ] No performance issues with many footprints\n- [ ] Unit tests pass\n\nFixes #360\n\nü§ñ Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)",

initial_alpha - (steps_taken * alpha_decay_rate)\n\talpha = maxf(alpha, 0.05)  # Minimum visible alpha\n\n\t# Get the facing direction (from model rotation, not movement)\n\tvar facing_direction := Ensure footprint renders above floor (z_index 0) but below characters\n\tfootprint.z_index = 1\n\n\t# Set which foot this is (left or right boot texture)\n\tif footprint.has_method(\"set_foot\"):\n\t\tfootprint.set_foot(_is_left_foot)\n\n\t# Alternate left/right foot by slightly offsetting perpendicular to facing direction\n\tvar perpendicular := facing_direction.rotated(PI / 2.0)\n\tvar foot_offset := 4.0 if _is_left_foot else -4.0\n\tfootprint.global_position += perpendicular * foot_offset\n\t_is_left_foot = not _is_left_foot\n\n\t# Set alpha using the footprint's method\n\tif footprint.has_method(\"set_alpha\"):\n\t\tfootprint.set_alpha(alpha)\n\telse:\n\t\tfootprint.modulate.a = alpha\n\n\t# Add to scene tree\n\tvar scene := When the player or an enemy steps into a blood puddle, bloody boot footprints appear behind them, becoming more transparent with each step until they disappear.\n\n### Key Features\n- **Blood puddle detection**: Characters detect when they step in blood via Area2D overlap\n- **Fading footprints**: Each consecutive footprint is more transparent than the previous\n- **Persistent decals**: Footprints do NOT fade over time (as per requirements)\n- **Unlimited count**: No maximum limit on footprints (as per requirements)\n- **Both characters**: Feature applies to both player and enemies\n- **Alternating feet**: Left/right foot alternation for realistic trail\n- **Facing direction rotation**: Footprints rotate based on character's facing direction (aim direction)\n- **No footprints on blood**: Footprints only spawn on floor without blood\n\n### Technical Implementation\n- New `BloodyFeetComponent` component attached to Player and Enemy scenes\n- New `BloodFootprint.tscn` scene for footprint decals\n- Updated `BloodDecal` script to add Area2D collision for puddle detection\n- Added unit tests for `BloodyFeetComponent`\n\n### Configuration (BloodyFeetComponent)\n| Property | Default | Description |\n|----------|---------|-------------|\n| `blood_steps_count` | 6 | Number of footprints before blood runs out |\n| `step_distance` | 30.0 | Pixels between footprint spawns |\n| `initial_alpha` | 0.8 | Alpha of first footprint |\n| `alpha_decay_rate` | 0.12 | Alpha reduction per step |\n| `footprint_scale` | 0.72 | Size multiplier for footprints |\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n#### Session 1 (2026-01-25)\n\n1. **C# Player Scene Missing Component**: The `BloodyFeetComponent` was only added to the GDScript Player scene, but `BuildingLevel.tscn` uses the C# Player scene (`scenes/characters/csharp/Player.tscn`). Added the component to the C# scene.\n\n2. **Blood Detector Not Following Character**: The Area2D blood detector was parented to the `BloodyFeetComponent` Node (which has no transform), causing it to stay at world position (0, 0) instead of following the character. Fixed by parenting the detector to the CharacterBody2D.\n\n#### Session 2 (2026-01-25)\n\n3. **Texture Cropping Issue**: Boot print textures (11x16 px) were being cropped at top/bottom when rotated. Added vertical padding by increasing texture height to 20px (11x20).\n\n4. **Footprint Rotation Direction**: Footprints were rotating based on movement direction instead of character facing direction. Now uses `PlayerModel` or `EnemyModel` global_rotation to match the direction the character is looking/aiming. Handles flipped sprites correctly (when aiming left, scale.y is negative).\n\n#### Session 3 (2026-01-25)\n\n5. **Footprint Rotation 90¬∞ Off**: Boot prints were oriented incorrectly relative to the character's facing direction. Added PI/2 (90 degrees clockwise) offset to the rotation calculation.\n\n6. **Footprints Too Large**: Reduced `footprint_scale` from 0.8 to 0.72 (10% smaller as requested).\n\n7. **Texture Still Being Cropped**: Expanded boot print texture canvas from 11x20 to 22x40 (2x original size) with transparent padding to prevent cropping during rotation.\n\n8. **Footprints Appearing on Blood**: Added `_is_on_blood_puddle()` check to prevent footprints from spawning when character is currently standing on a blood puddle. Footprints now only appear on floor without blood.\n\n### Debug Logging\n- Enabled `debug_logging = true` in scene files for testing\n- Added logging to `blood_decal.gd` for tracing puddle creation\n- Added periodic overlap check logging to `BloodyFeetComponent`\n\n### Files Changed\n- `scripts/components/bloody_feet_component.gd` - Main component (facing direction rotation, blood overlap check)\n- `scripts/effects/blood_footprint.gd` - Footprint decal script\n- `scenes/effects/BloodFootprint.tscn` - Footprint scene\n- `scripts/effects/blood_decal.gd` - Added puddle detection Area2D + logging\n- `scenes/characters/Player.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent (GDScript version)\n- `scenes/characters/csharp/Player.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent (C# version)\n- `scenes/objects/Enemy.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent\n- `assets/sprites/effects/boot_print_*.png` - Boot print textures (22x40 with 2x padding)\n- `tests/unit/test_bloody_feet_component.gd` - Unit tests\n- `docs/case-studies/issue-360/` - Case study with debugging analysis and game logs\n\n## Test plan\n\n- [ ] Player stepping in blood puddle triggers footprint spawning\n- [ ] Footprints fade in alpha with each step (not over time)\n- [ ] Footprints stop appearing after `blood_steps_count` steps\n- [ ] Stepping in blood again resets the footprint counter\n- [ ] Enemies also leave bloody footprints\n- [ ] Footprints rotate to match character facing direction (not movement)\n- [ ] Footprints rotated correctly (toe pointing in facing direction)\n- [ ] Texture not cropped at top/bottom when rotated\n- [ ] Footprints only appear on floor without blood\n- [ ] No performance issues with many footprints\n- [ ] Unit tests pass\n\nFixes #360\n\nü§ñ Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)\nEOF\n)\" 2>&1",
